								where aa.send_status in ('WAIT_ASSIGN','WAIT_FINISH_ASSIGN','WAIT_SENDED_ASSIGN') and (aa.web_status='WAIT_SELLER_SEND_GOODS' or aa.web_status in ('TRADE_FINISHED','TRADE_BUYER_SIGNED','TRADE_BUYER_SIGNED','WAIT_BUYER_CONFIRM_GOODS') and aa.WAIT_SENDED_ASSIGN='T')
								group by aa.buyer_nick,bb.prd_no,bb.sku_name having count(1)>1
							) as repeat2 on repeat2.buyer_nick=a.buyer_nick and repeat2.prd_no=`repeat`.prd_no and repeat2.sku_name=`repeat`.sku_name  where 1=1  and a.send_status in  ('WAIT_ASSIGN','WAIT_FINISH_ASSIGN','WAIT_SENDED_ASSIGN') AND a.exception_online=0  and  a.items_num = 1 and a.sku_num = 1  group by new_tid  order by payment_time desc  limit 0,100
